The housekeeper Xiao Fan contacted me the day before check-in, added WeChat, and asked about the check-in requirements and arrival time. When I checked in, I upgraded the room. Welcome fruit snacks and drinks were arranged. Special and considerate reminders were given that if you like drinks, they can be delivered to the room. I was slightly disappointed with the breakfast, which was still very different from Marriott Hyatt. In particular, there was no yogurt provided before 9 o'clock for breakfast. It was said that there was no yogurt, which was not very understandable, and the environment was also crowded.

Exit the subway station A/D exit, cross the road to the hotel, which is quite convenient. The room on the fifth floor is very quiet in the corridor, but it's a pity that the upper window is too long, which affects the scenery outside the window. The breakfast is OK, the regular star hotel buffet style, there are not many dishes that reflect the characteristics of Xi'an. I wanted to drink Hu La Tang, but it was a pity that there was no. The room is still good and spacious, but it's a pity that there is no floor-to-ceiling window, and the small window divides the scenery outside the window. The only drawback is that the door from the bathroom to the bedroom is semi-translucent, and it is very bright in the morning. Although the window in the bathroom has a lifting curtain that can be lowered, it is quite translucent in the morning. The curtains are drawn in the whole bedroom early in the morning, and it is dark and suitable for lazy sleep. It's the bathroom that is translucent, and there is no curtain to cover the door, so I was woken up by the light. The service in the front hall is very good. At 1 a.m., the sheets are uncomfortable. I contacted the front desk and they were quickly sent to replace them. The housekeeper, Ms. Zhao Guoyu, was very responsible. She confirmed the room before check-in and provided travel advice during the stay. The performance program list of the Never-Sleeping City and Furong Garden was very helpful to us. I will consider staying in this hotel again when I come to Xi'an next time.

Young brothers and sisters in Ming uniforms will guide you when you enter, pour chrysanthemum water to drink, help with luggage, and are very considerate during check-in. .

There is also a noodle shop opposite the hotel, Da Qin Noodle House, which is open late. The taste is very nice!

      The hotel facilities are very complete, including a gym, swimming pool, etc.~

The price is slightly higher and hotel guests can get discounts. It is very cost-effective if you go directly to the hotel for group purchase. The advantage is that it is very close to the hotel ~ it is very convenient to return and exchange clothes!

There are welcome refreshments, Ctrip points can be exchanged for fruit platters, and there is also a special turndown service and good night drinks. The bathing pool is large enough and the water temperature is very hot. Taking a bath at night can relieve the fatigue of the day's journey.
Check-in coincided with the peak of the Spring Festival holiday, and the hotel is located in the core of the scenic spot. There was a little hiccup when parking. I especially want to praise the doorman and security team leader who were on duty that day, especially the lobby manager who came up with various solutions in a timely manner and was calm. In response to emergencies, temporary parking spaces are set up on the hotel ground for guests to alleviate urgent needs and make people feel at home!
If you come to Xi'an again, you will definitely choose Furongge Hotel again. Highly recommended!
